<P class="p0 ft0">Regeringens proposition 2021/22:21</P>
<TABLE cellpadding=0 cellspacing=0 class="t0">
<TR>
	<TD class="tr0 td0"><SPAN class="p1 ft1">Skatteavtal mellan Sverige och Slovenien</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr0 td1"><SPAN class="p2 ft1">Prop.</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD class="tr1 td2"><SPAN class="p3 ft2">&nbsp;</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr1 td3"><SPAN class="p2 ft1">2021/22:21</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
<P class="p4 ft3">Regeringen verlmnar denna proposition till riksdagen.</P>
<P class="p5 ft3">Stockholm den 7 oktober 2021</P>
<P class="p6 ft4">Stefan Lfven</P>
<P class="p7 ft4">Magdalena Andersson <SPAN class="ft3">(Finansdepartementet)</SPAN></P>
<P class="p8 ft1">Propositionens huvudsakliga innehll</P>
<P class="p9 ft3">I propositionen fresls att riksdagen godknner ett skatteavtal mellan Sverige och Slovenien fr undvikande av dubbelbeskattning betrffande skatter p inkomst och p frmgenhet samt frhindrande av skatteflykt och skatteundandragande. Vidare fresls att riksdagen antar en lag om detta avtal. Lagen fresls trda i kraft den dag som regeringen bestmmer. Avtalet avser att erstta 1980 rs skatteavtal mellan Sverige och Jugoslavien svitt gller frhllandet mellan Sverige och Slovenien.</P>
<P class="p10 ft3">Det nya avtalet uppfyller nya internationella standarder som syftar till att motverka skatteflykt och skatteundandragande genom avtalsmissbruk.</P>
<P class="p11 ft3">ven informationsutbytet uppdateras till nu gllande internationella standarder.</P>
<P class="p12 ft3">I frga om beskattningsreglerna infrs bl.a. tydligare regler fr inkomster som uppbrs genom delgarbeskattade subjekt. Reglerna fr justering av inkomst vid felprissttning av transaktioner mellan fretag i intressegemenskap moderniseras. Beskattningen av pensioner och liknande utbetalningar ndras. En vergngsbestmmelse gr det dock mjligt fr den som omedelbart fre avtalets ikrafttrdande var mottagare av pension eller liknande utbetalning att fortstta lta sig beskattas enligt de gamla reglerna.</P>
<P class="p13 ft3">1</P>

	<TD rowspan=2 class="tr6 td12"><SPAN class="p19 ft1">1</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD rowspan=2 class="tr6 td13"><SPAN class="p20 ft1">Frslag till riksdagsbeslut</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr2 td14"><SPAN class="p3 ft3">Prop. 2021/22:21</SPAN> </TD>

	<TD class="tr7 td14"><SPAN class="p3 ft6">&nbsp;</SPAN> </TD>

<P class="p21 ft3">Regeringens frslag:</P>
<P class="p22 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft7">Riksdagen godknner avtalet mellan Konungariket Sverige och Republiken Slovenien fr undvikande av dubbelbeskattning betrffande skatter p inkomst och p frmgenhet samt frhindrande av skatteflykt och skatteundandragande.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p23 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft7">Riksdagen antar regeringens frslag till lag om skatteavtal mellan Sverige och Slovenien.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p24 ft3">3</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="page_4">
<DIV id="p4dimg1">
<INGENBILD zsrc="H903214x1.jpg/" id="p4img1">
</DIV>


<TABLE cellpadding=0 cellspacing=0 class="t3">
<TR>
	<TD class="tr2 td15"><SPAN class="p3 ft3">Prop. 2021/22:21</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD rowspan=2 class="tr8 td16"><SPAN class="p19 ft1">2</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD rowspan=2 class="tr8 td17"><SPAN class="p25 ft1">Frslag till lag om skatteavtal mellan</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD class="tr9 td15"><SPAN class="p3 ft8">&nbsp;</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
<P class="p26 ft1">Sverige och Slovenien</P>
<P class="p27 ft3">Hrigenom freskrivs fljande.</P>
<P class="p28 ft3"><SPAN class="ft9">1  </SPAN>Det avtal fr undvikande av dubbelbeskattning betrffande skatter p inkomst och p frmgenhet samt frhindrande av skatteflykt och skatteundandragande som Sverige och Slovenien undertecknade den 12 maj 2021 ska, tillsammans med det protokoll som r fogat till avtalet och utgr en del av detta, glla som lag hr i landet. Avtalet r avfattat p engelska. Den engelska texten och en svensk versttning av avtalet framgr av bilagan till denna lag.</P>
<P class="p29 ft3"><SPAN class="ft9">2  </SPAN>Avtalets beskattningsregler ska tillmpas endast till den del dessa medfr inskrnkning av den skattskyldighet i Sverige som annars skulle freligga.</P>
<P class="p30 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft10">Denna lag trder i kraft den dag som regeringen bestmmer.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p31 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft10">Lagen tillmpas frsta gngen i frga om</SPAN></P>
<P class="p32 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft11">kllskatter, p belopp som betalas eller tillgodofrs den 1 januari det r som fljer nrmast efter den dag d lagen trder i kraft eller senare,</SPAN></P>
<P class="p33 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft11">andra skatter p inkomst och p frmgenhet, p skatt som pfrs fr beskattningsr som brjar den 1 januari det r som fljer nrmast efter den dag d lagen trder i kraft eller senare, och</SPAN></P>
<P class="p33 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">c)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft11">informationsutbyte enligt artikel 25 i avtalet, p begran som framstlls den dag d lagen trder i kraft eller senare oavsett vilket r som beskattningsansprket hnfr sig till.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p34 ft3">3. Fljande frfattningar ska inte lngre tillmpas svitt avser frhllandet mellan Sverige och Slovenien</P>
<P class="p32 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft11">frordningen (1982:70) om dubbelbeskattningsavtal mellan Sverige och Jugoslavien,</SPAN></P>
<P class="p34 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft11">frordningen (1982:71) om kupongskatt fr person med hemvist i Jugoslavien, m.m.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p34 ft3">4. Frordningen (1982:70) om dubbelbeskattningsavtal mellan Sverige och Jugoslavien tillmpas dock fortfarande i frga om</P>
<P class="p32 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft11">kllskatter, p belopp som betalas eller tillgodofrs fre den 1 januari det r som fljer nrmast efter den dag d lagen trder i kraft, och</SPAN></P>
<P class="p33 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft11">andra skatter p inkomst och p frmgenhet, p skatt som pfrs fr beskattningsr som brjar fre den 1 januari det r som fljer nrmast efter den dag d lagen trder i kraft.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p33 ft3">5. Artikel 18 punkterna <NOBR>13</NOBR> i bilagan till frordningen (1982:70) om dubbelbeskattningsavtal mellan Sverige och Jugoslavien tillmpas fortfarande i frga om en fysisk person som omedelbart fre ikrafttrdandet av avtalet av den 12 maj 2021 var mottagare av betalning som omfattas av nmnda bestmmelser och denne, i enlighet med artikel 28 punkt 5 i avtalet har valt att dessa bestmmelser, och inte bestmmelserna i artikel 17 i avtalet, ska tillmpas p sdan betalning. De ldre bestmmelserna</P>
<P class="p35 ft3">4</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="page_5">


<DIV>
<DIV id="id_1">
<P class="p14 ft3">ska tillmpas frn och med det r d valet grs och till dess valet terkallas. Nr ett val har terkallats kan inget nytt val gras.</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_2">
<P class="p36 ft3">Prop. 2021/22:21</P>
<P class="p37 ft3">5</P>
</DIV>
</DIV>

	<TD class="tr4 td19"><SPAN class="p3 ft2">&nbsp;</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD colspan=3 class="tr4 td29"><SPAN class="p3 ft9">TEUNDANDRAGANDE</SPAN> </TD>

<DIV id="id_2">
<DIV id="id_2_1">
<P class="p41 ft3">The Kingdom of Sweden and the Republic of Slovenia,</P>
<P class="p42 ft3">Intending to conclude a Convention for the elimination of double taxation with respect to taxes on income and on capital without creating opportunities for <NOBR>non-taxation</NOBR> or reduced taxation through tax evasion or avoidance (including through <NOBR>treaty-shopping</NOBR> arrangements aimed at obtaining reliefs provided in this Convention for the indirect benefit of residents of third States),</P>
<P class="p43 ft3">Have agreed as follows:</P>
<P class="p44 ft9">Article 1</P>
<P class="p45 ft4">Persons covered</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_2_2">
<P class="p46 ft3">Konungariket Sverige och Republiken Slovenien,</P>
<P class="p47 ft3">som avser att ing avtal fr undvikande av dubbelbeskattning betrffande skatter p inkomst och p frmgenhet, utan att skapa frutsttningar fr <NOBR>icke-beskattning</NOBR> eller minskad skatt genom skatteflykt eller skatteundandragande (dri inbegripet genom s.k. treatyshopping, som syftar till att personer med hemvist i en stat som inte r part till detta avtal indirekt ska f frmner enligt detta avtal),</P>
<P class="p48 ft3">har kommit verens om fljande:</P>
<P class="p44 ft9">Artikel 1</P>
<P class="p45 ft4">Personer p vilka avtalet tillmpas</P>
</DIV>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_3">
<DIV id="id_3_1">
<P class="p49 ft12">1. This Convention shall apply to persons who are residents of one or</P>
<TABLE cellpadding=0 cellspacing=0 class="t5">
<TR>
	<TD class="tr5 td30"><SPAN class="p3 ft2">&nbsp;</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr5 td31"><SPAN class="p50 ft3">both of the Contracting States.</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD class="tr11 td30"><SPAN class="p3 ft2">&nbsp;</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr11 td31"><SPAN class="p17 ft3">2. For the purposes of this</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD class="tr4 td30"><SPAN class="p3 ft2">&nbsp;</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr4 td31"><SPAN class="p17 ft3">Convention, income derived by or</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD class="tr5 td30"><SPAN class="p3 ft2">&nbsp;</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr5 td31"><SPAN class="p17 ft3">through an entity or arrangement</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD class="tr4 td30"><SPAN class="p3 ft2">&nbsp;</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr4 td31"><SPAN class="p17 ft3">that is treated as wholly or partly</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD class="tr4 td30"><SPAN class="p3 ft2">&nbsp;</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr4 td31"><SPAN class="p17 ft3">fiscally transparent under the tax</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD class="tr5 td30"><SPAN class="p3 ft2">&nbsp;</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr5 td31"><SPAN class="p17 ft3">law of either Contracting State shall</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD class="tr4 td30"><SPAN class="p3 ft2">&nbsp;</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr4 td31"><SPAN class="p17 ft3">be considered to be income of a</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD class="tr4 td30"><SPAN class="p3 ft2">&nbsp;</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr4 td31"><SPAN class="p17 ft3">resident of a Contracting State but</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD class="tr5 td30"><SPAN class="p3 ft2">&nbsp;</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr5 td31"><SPAN class="p17 ft3">only to the extent that the income is</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD class="tr4 td30"><SPAN class="p51 ft3">6</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr4 td31"><SPAN class="p17 ft3">treated, for purposes of taxation by</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_3_2">
<P class="p52 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft10">Detta avtal tillmpas p personer som har hemvist i en avtalsslutande stat eller i bda avtalsslutande staterna.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p53 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft10">Vid tillmpningen av detta avtal ska inkomst som frvrvas av eller genom en person, som enligt skattelagstiftningen i ngon av de avtalsslutande staterna helt eller delvis r freml fr delgarbeskattning, anses frvrvad av en person med hemvist i en avtalsslutande stat till den del som inkomsten, enligt skattelagstift-</SPAN></P>
</DIV>
</DIV>
</DIV>
<DIV id="page_7">


<DIV id="id_1">
<DIV id="id_1_1">
<P class="p54 ft3">that State, as the income of a resident of that State. In no case shall the provisions of this paragraph be construed to affect a Contracting States right to tax the residents of that State.</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_1_2">
<P class="p14 ft3">ningen i denna stat, behandlas som Prop. 2021/22:21 inkomst hos en person med hemvist</P>
<P class="p55 ft3">i den staten. Bestmmelserna i denna punkt pverkar inte p ngot stt en avtalsslutande stats rtt att beskatta personer med hemvist i denna stat.</P>
</DIV>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_2">
<TABLE cellpadding=0 cellspacing=0 class="t6">
<TR>
	<TD class="tr2 td32"><SPAN class="p3 ft9">Article 2</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr2 td33"><SPAN class="p3 ft9">Artikel 2</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD class="tr10 td32"><SPAN class="p3 ft4">Taxes covered</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr10 td33"><SPAN class="p3 ft13">Skatter p vilka avtalet tillmpas</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_3">
<DIV id="id_3_1">
<P class="p56 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft10">This Convention shall apply to taxes on income and on capital imposed on behalf of a Contracting State or of its political subdivisions or local authorities, irrespective of the manner in which they are levied.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p57 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft10">There shall be regarded as taxes on income and on capital all taxes imposed on total income, on total capital, or on elements of income or of capital, including taxes on gains from the alienation of movable or immovable property, as well as taxes on capital appreciation.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p58 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">3.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft10">The existing taxes to which the Convention shall apply are in particular:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p59 ft3">a) in Slovenia:</P>
<P class="p56 ft3">(i) the tax on income of legal persons (davek od dohodkov pravnih oseb);</P>
<P class="p60 ft3">(ii) the tax on income of individuals (dohodnina); and</P>
<P class="p60 ft3">(iii) the tax on property (davek od premoenja)</P>
<P class="p61 ft3">(hereinafter referred to as Slovenian tax);</P>
<P class="p59 ft3">b) in Sweden:</P>
<P class="p61 ft3">(i) the national income tax (den statliga inkomstskatten);</P>
<P class="p60 ft3">(ii) the withholding tax on dividends (kupongskatten);</P>
<P class="p62 ft3">(iii) the income tax on nonresidents (den srskilda inkomstskatten fr utomlands bosatta);</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_3_2">
<P class="p63 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft11">Detta avtal tillmpas p skatter p inkomst och p frmgenhet som pfrs fr en avtalsslutande stats, dess politiska underavdelningars eller lokala myndigheters rkning, oberoende av det stt p vilket skatterna tas ut.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p64 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft11">Med skatter p inkomst och p frmgenhet frsts alla skatter som tas ut p inkomst eller frmgenhet i dess helhet eller p delar av inkomst eller frmgenhet, dri inbegripet skatter p vinst p grund av verltelse av ls eller fast egendom, samt skatter p vrdestegring.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p65 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">3.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft11">De fr nrvarande utgende skatter, p vilka detta avtal tillmpas, r srskilt:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p59 ft3">a) i Slovenien:</P>
<P class="p63 ft3">1) skatten p juridiska personers inkomst (davek od dohodkov pravnih oseb),</P>
<P class="p66 ft3">2) skatten p fysiska personers inkomst (dohodnina), och</P>
<P class="p66 ft3">3) skatten p egendom (davek od premoenja)</P>
<P class="p67 ft3">(i det fljande benmnda slovensk skatt),</P>
<P class="p59 ft3">b) i Sverige:</P>
<P class="p68 ft3">1) den statliga inkomstskatten,</P>
<P class="p69 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">2)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft10">kupongskatten,</SPAN></P>
<P class="p70 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">3)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft10">den srskilda inkomstskatten fr utomlands bosatta,</SPAN></P>
<P class="p71 ft3">7</P>
</DIV>
</DIV>
</DIV>

<P class="p89 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft10">As regards the application of the Convention at any time by a</SPAN></P>

<P class="p54 ft3">determined, or if he has not a permanent home available to him in either State, he shall be deemed to be a resident only of the State in which he has an habitual abode;</P>
<P class="p98 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">c)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft10">if he has an habitual abode in both States or in neither of them, he shall be deemed to be a resident only of the State of which he is a national;</SPAN></P>
<P class="p99 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">d)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft10">if he is a national of both States or of neither of them, the competent authorities of the Contracting States shall settle the question by mutual agreement.</SPAN></P>

<DIV id="id_1_2">
<P class="p14 ft3">levnadsintressen eller om han inte i Prop. 2021/22:21 ngondera staten har en bostad som</P>
<P class="p55 ft3">stadigvarande str till hans frfogande, anses han ha hemvist endast i den stat dr han stadigvarande vistas,</P>
<P class="p100 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">c)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft10">om han stadigvarande vistas i bda staterna eller om han inte vistas stadigvarande i ngon av dem, anses han ha hemvist endast i den stat dr han r medborgare,</SPAN></P>
<P class="p101 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">d)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft10">om han r medborgare i bda staterna eller om han inte r medborgare i ngon av dem, ska de behriga myndigheterna i de avtalsslutande staterna avgra frgan genom msesidig verenskommelse.</SPAN></P>

<P class="p89 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">3.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft11">A building site or a construction, assembly or installation project or supervisory activities in connection therewith constitutes a permanent establishment only if such site, project or activities last more than twelve months.</SPAN></P>

<DIV id="id_2">
<DIV id="id_2_1">
<P class="p89 ft12"><SPAN class="ft3">8.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft15">The fact that a company which is a resident of a Contracting State controls or is controlled by a company which is a resident of the other Contracting State, or which carries on business in that other State (whether through a permanent establishment or otherwise), shall not of itself constitute either company a permanent establishment of the other.</SPAN></P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_2_2">
<P class="p52 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">8.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft10">Den omstndigheten att ett bolag med hemvist i en avtalsslutande stat kontrollerar eller kontrolleras av ett bolag med hemvist i den andra avtalsslutande staten eller ett bolag som bedriver affrsverksamhet i denna andra stat (antingen frn fast driftstlle eller p annat stt) medfr inte i sig att ngotdera bolaget utgr fast driftstlle fr det andra.</SPAN></P>
</DIV>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_3">
<P class="p14 ft3">14</P>
</DIV>
</DIV>
<DIV id="page_15">


<DIV id="id_1">
<DIV id="id_1_1">
<P class="p89 ft12"><SPAN class="ft3">9.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft14">For the purposes of this Ar- ticle, an enterprise is closely related to an enterprise if, based on all the relevant facts and circumstances, one has control of the other or both are under the control of the same persons or enterprises. In any case, an enterprise shall be considered to be closely related to an enterprise if one possesses directly or indirectly more than 50 per cent of the beneficial interest in the other (or, in the case of a company, more than 50 per cent of the aggregate vote and value of the companys shares or of the beneficial equity interest in the company) or if another person or enterprise possesses directly or indirectly more than 50 per cent of the beneficial interest (or, in the case of a company, more than 50 per cent of the aggregate vote and value of the companys shares or of the beneficial equity interest in the company) in the two enterprises.</SPAN></P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_1_2">
<P class="p104 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">9.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft11">Vi tillmpningen av denna Prop. 2021/22:21 artikel ska ett fretag anses nrst-</SPAN></P>
<P class="p55 ft3">ende till ett fretag om, med beaktande av alla relevanta fakta och omstndigheter, det ena kontrollerar det andra eller bda fretagen kontrolleras av samma personer eller fretag. Ett fretag anses under alla omstndigheter vara nrstende till ett fretag om det ena direkt eller indirekt innehar mer n 50 procent av garandelarna i det andra (eller, i frga om ett bolag, mer n 50 procent av det sammanlagda rstetalet och vrdet av bolagets andelar eller aktiekapital) eller om en person eller ett annat fretag direkt eller indirekt innehar mer n 50 procent av garandelarna (eller, i frga om ett bolag, mer n 50 procent av det sammanlagda rstetalet och vrdet av bolagets andelar eller aktiekapital) i bda fretagen.</P>
</DIV>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_2">

<P class="p89 ft12"><SPAN class="ft3">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft14">Income derived by a resident of a Contracting State from immovable property (including income from agriculture or forestry) situated in the other Contracting State may be taxed in that other State.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p105 ft12"><SPAN class="ft3">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft14">The term immovable property shall have the meaning which it has under the law of the Contracting State in which the property in question is situated. The term shall in any case include property accessory to immovable property, livestock and equipment used in agriculture and forestry, rights to which the provisions of general law respecting landed property apply, buildings, usufruct of immovable property and rights to variable or</SPAN></P>

<DIV id="id_1_1">
<P class="p90 ft3">Prop. 2021/22:21 fixed payments as consideration for the working of, or the right to work, mineral deposits, sources and other natural resources; ships and aircraft shall not be regarded as immovable property.</P>

<DIV id="id_1_2">
<P class="p54 ft3">eller rtten att nyttja mineralfrekomst, klla eller annan naturtillgng. Skepp och luftfartyg anses inte vara fast egendom.</P>

<DIV id="id_2">
<DIV id="id_2_1">
<P class="p89 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">3.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft11">The provisions of paragraph 1 shall apply to income derived from the direct use, letting, or use in any other form of immovable property.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p105 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">4.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft11">The provisions of paragraphs 1 and 3 shall also apply to the income from immovable property of an enterprise.</SPAN></P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_2_2">
<P class="p52 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">3.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft10">Bestmmelserna i punkt 1 tillmpas p inkomst som frvrvas genom omedelbart brukande, uthyrning eller annan anvndning av fast egendom.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p108 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">4.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft10">Bestmmelserna i punkterna 1 och 3 tillmpas ven p inkomst av fast egendom som tillhr fretag.</SPAN></P>

<DIV id="id_2">
<DIV id="id_2_1">
<P class="p115 ft3">1. Where</P>
<P class="p116 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft16">an enterprise of a Contracting State participates directly or indirectly in the management, control or capital of an enterprise of the other Contracting State, or</SPAN></P>
<P class="p117 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft11">the same persons participate directly or indirectly in the management, control or capital of an enterprise of a Contracting State and an enterprise of the other Contracting State,</SPAN></P>
<P class="p118 ft3">and in either case conditions are made or imposed between the two enterprises in their commercial or financial relations which differ from those which would be made between independent enterprises, then any profits which would, but for those conditions, have accrued to one of the enterprises, but, by reason of those conditions, have not so accrued, may be included in the profits of that enterprise and taxed accordingly.</P>

	<TD class="tr4 td61"><SPAN class="p3 ft2">&nbsp;</SPAN> </TD>

	<TD colspan=4 class="tr5 td31"><SPAN class="p17 ft3">profits if that other State considers</SPAN> </TD>

	<TD class="tr4 td61"><SPAN class="p51 ft3">18</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD colspan=2 class="tr4 td98"><SPAN class="p91 ft3">the adjustment</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr4 td46"><SPAN class="p120 ft3">justified. In</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr4 td50"><SPAN class="p17 ft3">deter-</SPAN> </TD>

<DIV id="id_2_2">
<P class="p121 ft3">1. I fall d:</P>
<P class="p122 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft16">ett fretag i en avtalsslutande stat direkt eller indirekt deltar i ledningen eller kontrollen av ett fretag i den andra avtalsslutande staten eller ger del i detta fretags kapital, eller</SPAN></P>
<P class="p123 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft10">samma personer direkt eller indirekt deltar i ledningen eller kontrollen av svl ett fretag i en avtalsslutande stat som ett fretag i den andra avtalsslutande staten eller ger del i bda dessa fretags kapital, iakttas fljande.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p124 ft3">Om mellan fretagen i frga om handelsfrbindelser eller finansiella frbindelser avtalas eller freskrivs villkor, som avviker frn dem som skulle ha avtalats mellan av varandra oberoende fretag, fr all inkomst, som utan sdana villkor skulle ha tillkommit det ena fretaget men som p grund av villkoren i frga inte tillkommit detta fretag, inrknas i detta fretags inkomst och beskattas i verensstmmelse drmed.</P>
<P class="p125 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft10">I fall d en avtalsslutande stat i inkomsten fr ett fretag i denna stat inrknar  och i verensstmmelse drmed beskattar  inkomst, fr vilken ett fretag i den andra avtalsslutande staten beskattats i denna andra stat, samt den slunda inrknade inkomsten r sdan som skulle ha tillkommit fretag i den frstnmnda staten om de villkor som avtalats mellan fretagen hade varit sdana som skulle ha avtalats mellan av varandra oberoende fretag, ska denna andra stat genomfra vederbrlig justering av det skattebelopp som pfrts inkomsten dr, under frutsttning att denna andra stat anser att justeringen r berttigad. Vid sdan justering iakttas</SPAN></P>
</DIV>
</DIV>
</DIV>
<DIV id="page_19">


<DIV id="id_1">
<DIV id="id_1_1">
<P class="p54 ft3">mining such adjustment, due regard shall be had to the other provisions of this Convention and the competent authorities of the Contracting States shall if necessary consult each other.</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_1_2">
<P class="p14 ft3">vriga bestmmelser i detta avtal Prop. 2021/22:21 och de behriga myndigheterna i de</P>
<P class="p126 ft3">avtalsslutande staterna ska vid behov verlgga med varandra.</P>
</DIV>

<DIV id="id_2">
<TABLE cellpadding=0 cellspacing=0 class="t17">
<TR>
	<TD class="tr2 td32"><SPAN class="p3 ft9">Article 10</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr2 td105"><SPAN class="p3 ft17">Artikel 10</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD class="tr10 td32"><SPAN class="p3 ft4">Dividends</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr10 td105"><SPAN class="p3 ft4">Utdelning</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>

<DIV id="id_3">
<DIV id="id_3_1">
<P class="p127 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft10">Dividends paid by a company which is a resident of a Contracting State to a resident of the other Contracting State may be taxed in that other State.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p98 ft12"><SPAN class="ft3">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft14">However, dividends paid by a company which is a resident of a Contracting State may also be taxed in that State according to the laws of that State, but if the beneficial owner of the dividends is a resident of the other Contracting State, the tax so charged shall not exceed:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p128 ft3">a) 5 per cent of the gross amount of the dividends if the beneficial owner is a company which holds directly at least 25 per cent of the capital or controls directly at least 25 per cent of the voting power of the company paying the dividends throughout a 365 day period that includes the day of the payment of the dividend (for the purpose of computing that period, no account shall be taken of changes of ownership that would directly result from a corporate reorganisation, such as a merger or divisive reorganisation, of the company that holds the shares or that pays the dividend);</P>
<P class="p129 ft3">b) 15 per cent of the gross amount of the dividends in all other cases.</P>
<P class="p130 ft3">This paragraph shall not affect the taxation of the company in respect of the profits out of which the dividends are paid.</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_3_2">
<P class="p131 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft11">Utdelning frn bolag med hemvist i en avtalsslutande stat till person med hemvist i den andra avtalsslutande staten fr beskattas i denna andra stat.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p132 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft11">Utdelning frn bolag med hemvist i en avtalsslutande stat fr emellertid beskattas ven i den staten, enligt lagstiftningen i denna stat, men om den som har rtt till utdelningen har hemvist den andra avtalsslutande staten fr skatten inte verstiga:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p133 ft3">a) 5 procent av utdelningens bruttobelopp om den som har rtt till utdelningen r ett bolag som direkt innehar minst 25 procent av kapitalet eller direkt kontrollerar minst 25 procent av rstetalet i det utdelande bolaget under en period om 365 dagar som innefattar den dag d utdelningen betalas ut (vid berkningen av denna period beaktas inte frndringar i gande som direkt fljer av en omstrukturering, ssom fusion eller fission av det bolag som innehar aktierna eller betalar utdelningen),</P>
<P class="p134 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft10">15 procent av utdelningens bruttobelopp i vriga fall.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p135 ft3">Denna punkt berr inte bolagets beskattning fr den vinst av vilken utdelningen betalas.</P>
<P class="p136 ft3">19</P>

<P class="p89 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">4.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft11">The provisions of paragraphs 1 and 2 shall not apply if the beneficial owner of the dividends, being a resident of a Contracting State, carries on business in the other Contracting State of which the company paying the dividends is a resident through a permanent establishment situated therein and the holding in respect of which the dividends are paid is effectively connected with such permanent establishment. In such case the provisions of Article 7 shall apply.</SPAN></P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_2_2">
<P class="p52 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">4.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft10">Bestmmelserna i punkterna 1 och 2 tillmpas inte, om den som har rtt till utdelningen har hemvist</SPAN></P>
<P class="p139 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">i</SPAN><SPAN class="ft10">en avtalsslutande stat och bedriver rrelse i den andra avtalsslutande staten, dr bolaget som betalar utdelningen har hemvist, frn dr belget fast driftstlle, samt den andel p grund av vilken utdelningen betalas ger verkligt samband med det fasta driftstllet. I sdant fall tillmpas bestmmelserna i artikel 7.</SPAN></P>

	<TD class="tr2 td132"><SPAN class="p3 ft9">Artikel 11</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr2 td14"><SPAN class="p3 ft3">Prop. 2021/22:21</SPAN> </TD>

	<TD class="tr10 td32"><SPAN class="p3 ft4">Interest</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr10 td132"><SPAN class="p3 ft4">Rnta</SPAN> </TD>

<DIV id="id_2">
<DIV id="id_2_1">
<P class="p89 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft10">Interest arising in a Contracting State and paid to a resident of the other Contracting State may be taxed in that other State.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p143 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft10">However, interest arising in a Contracting State may also be taxed in that State according to the laws of that State, but if the beneficial owner of the interest is a resident of the other Contracting State, the tax so charged shall not exceed 5 per cent of the gross amount of the interest.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p144 ft12"><SPAN class="ft3">3.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft14">Notwithstanding the provisions of paragraph 2 interest, mentioned in paragraph 1, shall be taxable only in the Contracting State of which the beneficial owner of the interest is a resident if one of the following requirements is fulfilled:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p128 ft12">a) the payer or the recipient of the interest is the Contracting State itself, a governmental body or agency, a political subdivision or a local authority thereof or the Central Bank of a Contracting State;</P>
<P class="p145 ft3">b) the interest is paid with respect to a loan made, guaranteed or insured, or a credit extended, guaranteed or insured by an institution of the other Contacting State with the objective to promote exports or development;</P>
<P class="p146 ft12">c) the interest is paid in respect of an indebtedness arising on the sale on credit of any merchandise or industrial, commercial or scientific equipment to an enterprise of the other Contracting State.</P>
<P class="p147 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">4.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft10">The term interest as used in this Article means income from </SPAN><NOBR>debt-claims</NOBR> of every kind, whether or not secured by mortgage and</P>

<DIV id="id_2">
<DIV id="id_2_1">
<P class="p89 ft12"><SPAN class="ft3">6.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft15">Interest shall be deemed to arise in a Contracting State when the payer is a resident of that State. Where, however, the person paying the interest, whether he is a resident of a Contracting State or not, has in a Contracting State a permanent establishment in connection with which the indebtedness on which the interest is paid was incurred, and such interest is borne by such permanent establishment, then such interest shall be deemed to arise in the State in which the permanent establishment is situated.</SPAN></P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_2_2">
<P class="p52 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">6.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft10">Rnta anses hrrra frn en avtalsslutande stat om utbetalaren r en person med hemvist i denna stat. Om emellertid den person som betalar rntan, antingen han har hemvist i en avtalsslutande stat eller inte, i en avtalsslutande stat har ett fast driftstlle i samband med vilket den skuld uppkommit fr vilken rntan betalas, och rntan belastar det fasta driftstllet, anses rntan hrrra frn den stat dr det fasta driftstllet finns.</SPAN></P>
</DIV>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_3">
<DIV id="id_3_1">
<TABLE cellpadding=0 cellspacing=0 class="t19">
<TR>
	<TD class="tr2 td61"><SPAN class="p3 ft2">&nbsp;</SPAN> </TD>

<DIV id="id_3_2">
<P class="p52 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">7.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft10">D p grund av srskilda frbindelser mellan utbetalaren och den som har rtt till rntan eller mellan dem bda och annan person, rntebeloppet, med hnsyn till den fordran fr vilken rntan betalas, verstiger det belopp som skulle ha avtalats mellan utbetalaren och den</SPAN></P>
</DIV>
</DIV>
</DIV>
<DIV id="page_23">


<DIV id="id_1">
<DIV id="id_1_1">
<P class="p54 ft3">agreed upon by the payer and the beneficial owner in the absence of such relationship, the provisions of this Article shall apply only to the <NOBR>last-mentioned</NOBR> amount. In such case, the excess part of the payments shall remain taxable according to the laws of each Contracting State, due regard being had to the other provisions of this Convention.</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_1_2">
<P class="p14 ft3">som har rtt till rntan om sdana Prop. 2021/22:21 frbindelser inte frelegat, tillm-</P>
<P class="p55 ft3">pas bestmmelserna i denna artikel endast p sistnmnda belopp. I sdant fall beskattas verskjutande belopp enligt lagstiftningen i vardera avtalsslutande staten med iakttagande av vriga bestmmelser i detta avtal.</P>
</DIV>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_2">
<TABLE cellpadding=0 cellspacing=0 class="t17">
<TR>
	<TD class="tr2 td32"><SPAN class="p3 ft9">Article 12</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr2 td105"><SPAN class="p3 ft17">Artikel 12</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD class="tr10 td32"><SPAN class="p3 ft4">Royalties</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr10 td105"><SPAN class="p3 ft4">Royalty</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_3">
<DIV id="id_3_1">
<P class="p89 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft10">Royalties arising in a Contracting State and paid to a resident of the other Contracting State may be taxed in that other State.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p143 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft10">However, royalties arising in a Contracting State may also be taxed in that State according to the laws of that State, but if the beneficial owner of the royalties is a resident of the other Contracting State, the tax so charged shall not exceed 5 per cent of the gross amount of the royalties.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p144 ft12"><SPAN class="ft3">3.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft14">The term royalties as used in this Article means payments of any kind received as a consideration for the use of, or the right to use, any copyright of literary, artistic or scientific work including cinematograph films, any patent, trade mark, design or model, plan, secret formula or process, or for information concerning industrial, commercial or scientific experience.</SPAN></P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_3_2">
<P class="p63 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft11">Royalty som hrrr frn en avtalsslutande stat och som betalas till en person med hemvist i den andra avtalsslutande staten, fr beskattas i denna andra stat.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p150 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft11">Royalty fr emellertid beskattas ven i den avtalsslutande stat frn vilken den hrrr, enligt lagstiftningen i denna stat, men om den som har rtt till rntan har hemvist i den andra avtalsslutande</SPAN></P>
<P class="p151 ft3">staten fr skatten inte verstiga</P>
<P class="p152 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">5</SPAN><SPAN class="ft18">procent av royaltyns bruttobelopp.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p153 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">3.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft11">Med uttrycket royalty frsts i denna artikel varje slags betalning som tas emot ssom ersttning fr nyttjandet av eller fr rtten att nyttja upphovsrtt till litterrt, konstnrligt eller vetenskapligt verk, hri inbegripet biograffilm, patent, varumrke, mnster eller modell, ritning, hemligt recept eller hemlig tillverkningsmetod samt fr upplysning om erfarenhetsrn av industriell, kommersiell eller vetenskaplig natur.</SPAN></P>
</DIV>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_4">
<DIV id="id_4_1">
<P class="p89 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">4.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft10">The provisions of paragraphs 1 and 2 shall not apply if the beneficial owner of the royalties, being a resident of a Contracting State, carries on business in the other</SPAN></P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_4_2">
<P class="p103 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">4.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft11">Bestmmelserna i punkt 1 och 2 tillmpas inte om den som har rtt till royaltyn har hemvist i en avtalsslutande stat och bedriver rrelse i</SPAN></P>
<TABLE cellpadding=0 cellspacing=0 class="t20">
<TR>
	<TD class="tr5 td111"><SPAN class="p3 ft3">den andra avtalsslutande staten,</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr5 td112"><SPAN class="p17 ft3">23</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
</DIV>
</DIV>
</DIV>
<DIV id="page_24">


<DIV id="id_1">
<DIV id="id_1_1">
<P class="p90 ft3">Prop. 2021/22:21 Contracting State in which the royalties arise through a permanent establishment situated therein and the right or property in respect of which the royalties are paid is effectively connected with such permanent establishment. In such case the provisions of Article 7 shall apply.</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_1_2">
<P class="p54 ft3">frn vilken royaltyn hrrr, frn dr belget fast driftstlle, samt den rttighet eller egendom i frga om vilken royaltyn betalas ger verkligt samband med det fasta driftstllet. I sdant fall tillmpas bestmmelserna i artikel 7.</P>
</DIV>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_2">
<DIV id="id_2_1">
<P class="p89 ft12"><SPAN class="ft3">5.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft15">Royalties shall be deemed to arise in a Contracting State when the payer is a resident of that State. Where, however, the person paying the royalties, whether he is a resident of a Contracting State or not, has in a Contracting State a permanent establishment in connection with which the liability to pay the royalties was incurred, and such royalties are borne by such permanent establishment, then such royalties shall be deemed to arise in the State in which the permanent establishment is situated.</SPAN></P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_2_2">
<P class="p52 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">5.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft10">Royalty anses hrrra frn en avtalsslutande stat om utbetalaren r en person med hemvist i denna stat. Om, emellertid, den person som betalar royaltyn, antingen han har hemvist i en avtalsslutande stat eller inte, i en avtalsslutande stat har fast driftstlle i samband varmed skyldigheten att betala royaltyn uppkommit, och royaltyn belastar det fasta driftstllet, anses royaltyn hrrra frn den stat dr det fasta driftstllet finns.</SPAN></P>
</DIV>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_3">
<DIV id="id_3_1">
<P class="p89 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">6.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft11">Where, by reason of a special relationship between the payer and the beneficial owner or between both of them and some other person, the amount of the royalties, having regard to the use, right or information for which they are paid, exceeds the amount which would have been agreed upon by the payer and the beneficial owner in the absence of such relationship, the provisions of this Article shall apply only to the </SPAN><NOBR>last-mentioned</NOBR> amount. In such case, the excess part of the payments shall remain taxable according to the laws of each Contracting State, due regard being had to the other provisions of this Convention.</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_3_2">
<P class="p52 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">6.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft10">D p grund av srskilda frbindelser mellan utbetalaren och den som har rtt till royaltyn eller mellan dem bda och annan person, royaltybeloppet, med hnsyn till det nyttjande, den rttighet eller den upplysning fr vilken royaltyn betalas, verstiger det belopp som skulle ha avtalats mellan utbetalaren och den som har rtt till royaltyn om sdana frbindelser inte frelegat, tillmpas bestmmelserna i denna artikel endast p sistnmnda belopp. I sdant fall beskattas verskjutande belopp enligt lagstiftningen i vardera avtalsslutande staten med iakttagande av vriga bestmmelser i detta avtal.</SPAN></P>
</DIV>
</DIV>

<DIV id="id_2_1">
<P class="p89 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">3.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft10">Gains that an enterprise of a Contracting State that operates ships or aircraft in international traffic derives from the alienation of such ships or aircraft, or of movable property pertaining to the operation of such ships or aircraft, shall be taxable only in that State.</SPAN></P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_2_2">

<DIV id="id_4_1">
<P class="p89 ft12"><SPAN class="ft3">6.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft14">Notwithstanding the provisions of paragraph 5, gains from the alienation of any property derived</SPAN></P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_4_2">
<TABLE cellpadding=0 cellspacing=0 class="t9">
<TR>
	<TD class="tr2 td111"><SPAN class="p106 ft3">6. Vinst p grund av verltelse</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr2 td112"><SPAN class="p3 ft2">&nbsp;</SPAN> </TD>

<TR>
	<TD class="tr4 td111"><SPAN class="p106 ft3">av tillgng, som frvrvas av en</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr4 td112"><SPAN class="p3 ft2">&nbsp;</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD class="tr5 td111"><SPAN class="p106 ft3">fysisk person som har haft hemvist</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr5 td112"><SPAN class="p17 ft3">25</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>

<DIV id="page_26">


<DIV id="id_1">
<DIV id="id_1_1">
<P class="p90 ft12">Prop. 2021/22:21 by an individual who has been a resident of a Contracting State and who has become a resident of the other Contracting State, may be taxed in the <NOBR>first-mentioned</NOBR> State if the alienation of the property occurs at any time during the ten years next following the date on which the individual has ceased to be a resident of the <NOBR>first-mentioned</NOBR> State. The gain so taxed shall not include the gain, if any, that accrues during the period during which the individual is or was a resident of the other Contracting State.</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_1_2">
<P class="p54 ft3">i en avtalsslutande stat och som ftt hemvist i den andra avtalsslutande staten, fr  utan hinder av bestmmelserna i punkt 5  beskattas i den frstnmnda staten, om verltelsen sker vid ngot tillflle under de tio r som fljer nrmast efter den tidpunkt d den fysiska personen har upphrt att ha hemvist i den frstnmnda staten. Sdan vinst ska dock inte inkludera eventuell vinst som har uppkommit under den tid personen har haft hemvist i den andra avtalsslutande staten.</P>
</DIV>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_2">
<DIV id="id_2_1">
<P class="p155 ft9">Article 14</P>
<P class="p156 ft4">Income from employment</P>
<P class="p157 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft11">Subject to the provisions of Articles 15, 17 and 18 salaries, wages and other similar remuneration derived by a resident of a Contracting State in respect of an employment shall be taxable only in that State unless the employment is exercised in the other Contracting State. If the employment is so exercised, such remuneration as is derived therefrom may be taxed in that other State.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p158 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft11">Notwithstanding the provisions of paragraph 1, remuneration derived by a resident of a Contracting State in respect of an employment exercised in the other Contracting State shall be taxable only in the </SPAN><NOBR>first-mentioned</NOBR> State if:</P>
<P class="p159 ft3">a) the recipient is present in the other State for a period or periods not exceeding in the aggregate 183 days in any twelve month period commencing or ending in the fiscal year concerned, and</P>
<P class="p160 ft12">b) the remuneration is paid by, or on behalf of, an employer who is not a resident of the other State, and</P>
<P class="p154 ft3">26</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_2_2">
<P class="p14 ft9">Artikel 14</P>
<P class="p45 ft4">Inkomst av anstllning</P>
<P class="p161 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft10">Om inte bestmmelserna i artiklarna 15, 17 och 18 franleder annat, beskattas ln och annan liknande ersttning som person med hemvist i en avtalsslutande stat uppbr p grund av anstllning, endast i denna stat, svida inte arbetet utfrs i den andra avtalsslutande staten. Om arbetet utfrs i denna andra stat, fr ersttning som uppbrs fr arbetet beskattas dr.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p162 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft10">Utan hinder av bestmmelserna i punkt 1 beskattas ersttning, som person med hemvist i en avtalsslutande stat uppbr fr arbete i den andra avtalsslutande staten, endast i den frstnmnda staten, om:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p163 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft10">mottagaren vistas i den andra staten under tidsperiod eller tidsperioder som sammanlagt inte verstiger 183 dagar under en tolvmnadersperiod som brjar eller slutar under beskattningsret i frga,</SPAN></P>
<P class="p123 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft10">ersttningen betalas av arbetsgivare som inte har hemvist i den andra staten eller p dennes vgnar, och</SPAN></P>
</DIV>
</DIV>
</DIV>
<DIV id="page_27">


<DIV id="id_1">
<DIV id="id_1_1">
<P class="p127 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">c)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft10">the remuneration is not borne by a permanent establishment which the employer has in the other State.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p164 ft12"><SPAN class="ft3">3.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft14">Notwithstanding the preceding provisions of this Article and Ar- ticle 1, remuneration derived by an individual, whether a resident of a Contracting State or not, in respect of an employment, as a member of the regular complement of a ship or aircraft, that is exercised aboard a ship or aircraft operated in international traffic by an enterprise of a Contracting State shall be taxable only in that Contracting State. Where, however, such remuneration is derived by a resident of the other Contracting State, it may also be taxed in that other State.</SPAN></P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_1_2">
<P class="p165 ft3">c) ersttningen inte belastar fast Prop. 2021/22:21 driftstlle som arbetsgivaren har i</P>
<P class="p14 ft3">den andra staten.</P>
<P class="p166 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">3.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft11">Utan hinder av fregende bestmmelser i denna artikel och artikel 1 ska ersttning som en fysisk person  oavsett om personen har hemvist i en avtalsslutande stat eller inte  uppbr fr arbete i anstllning som medlem i besttningen ombord p skepp eller luftfartyg som ett fretag i en avtalsslutande stat anvnder i internationell trafik, beskattas endast i denna stat. I fall d sdan ersttning emellertid uppbrs av en person med hemvist i den andra avtalsslutande staten, fr ersttningen beskattas ven i denna andra stat.</SPAN></P>
</DIV>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_2">
<TABLE cellpadding=0 cellspacing=0 class="t23">
<TR>
	<TD class="tr2 td32"><SPAN class="p3 ft9">Article 15</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr2 td116"><SPAN class="p3 ft9">Artikel 15</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD class="tr10 td32"><SPAN class="p3 ft4">Directors fees</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr10 td116"><SPAN class="p3 ft13">Styrelsearvode</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_3">
<DIV id="id_3_1">
<P class="p89 ft3">Directors fees and other similar payments derived by a resident of a Contracting State in his capacity as a member of the board of directors or of a similar organ of a company which is a resident of the other Contracting State may be taxed in that other State.</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_3_2">
<P class="p89 ft3">Styrelsearvode och annan liknande ersttning, som person med hemvist i en avtalsslutande stat uppbr i egenskap av medlem i styrelse eller annat liknande organ i bolag med hemvist i den andra avtalsslutande staten, fr beskattas i denna andra stat.</P>
</DIV>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_4">
<TABLE cellpadding=0 cellspacing=0 class="t24">
<TR>
	<TD class="tr2 td32"><SPAN class="p3 ft9">Article 16</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr2 td139"><SPAN class="p3 ft9">Artikel 16</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD class="tr10 td32"><SPAN class="p3 ft4">Entertainers and sportspersons</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr10 td139"><SPAN class="p3 ft13">Artister och sportutvare</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_5">
<DIV id="id_5_1">
<P class="p89 ft12"><SPAN class="ft3">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft14">Notwithstanding the provisions of Article 14, income derived by a resident of a Contracting State as an entertainer, such as a theatre, motion picture, radio or television artiste, or a musician, or as a sportsperson, from that residents personal activities as such exercised in the other Contracting State, may be taxed in that other State.</SPAN></P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_5_2">
<P class="p131 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft11">Utan hinder av bestmmelserna i artikel 14 fr inkomst, som person med hemvist i en avtalsslutande stat frvrvar genom sin personliga verksamhet i den andra avtalsslutande staten i egenskap av artist, ssom teater- eller filmskdespelare, radio- eller televisionsartist eller musiker, eller i egenskap av sportutvare, beskattas i denna andra stat.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p167 ft3">27</P>
</DIV>
</DIV>
</DIV>
<DIV id="page_28">


<DIV id="id_1">
<DIV id="id_1_1">
<P class="p90 ft3">Prop. 2021/22:21 2. Where income in respect of personal activities exercised by an entertainer or a sportsperson acting as such accrues not to the entertainer or sportsperson but to another person, that income may, notwithstanding the provisions of Article 14, be taxed in the Contracting State in which the activities of the entertainer or sportsperson are exercised.</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_1_2">
<P class="p52 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft10">I fall d inkomst genom personlig verksamhet som artist eller sportutvare bedriver i denna egenskap inte tillfaller artisten eller sportutvaren sjlv utan annan person, fr denna inkomst, utan hinder av bestmmelserna i artikel 14, beskattas i den avtalsslutande stat dr artisten eller sportutvaren bedriver verksamheten.</SPAN></P>
</DIV>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_2">
<TABLE cellpadding=0 cellspacing=0 class="t25">
<TR>
	<TD class="tr2 td39"><SPAN class="p3 ft9">Article 17</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr2 td23"><SPAN class="p3 ft9">Artikel 17</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD class="tr10 td39"><SPAN class="p3 ft4">Pensions, annuities and similar</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr10 td23"><SPAN class="p3 ft4">Pension, livrnta och liknande</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
<TR>
	<TD class="tr4 td39"><SPAN class="p3 ft4">payments</SPAN> </TD>

<DIV id="id_3">
<DIV id="id_3_1">
<P class="p89 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft11">Pensions and other similar remuneration (including annuities) arising in a Contracting State and disbursements under the Social Security legislation of a Contracting State, paid to a resident of the other Contracting State may be taxed in the </SPAN><NOBR>first-mentioned</NOBR> Contracting State.</P>
<P class="p168 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft11">The term annuity means a stated sum payable periodically at stated times during life or during a specified or ascertainable period of time under an obligation to make the payments in return for adequate and full consideration in money or money's worth.</SPAN></P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_3_2">
<P class="p52 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft10">Pension och annan liknande ersttning (inklusive livrnta) som hrrr frn en avtalsslutande stat samt utbetalningar enligt socialfrskringslagstiftningen i en avtalsslutande stat, som betalas till en person med hemvist i den andra avtalsslutande staten, fr beskattas i den frstnmnda staten.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p169 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft10">Med uttrycket livrnta frsts ett faststllt belopp, som utbetalas periodiskt p faststllda tider under en persons livstid eller under angiven eller faststllbar tidsperiod och som utgr p grund av frpliktelse att verkstlla dessa utbetalningar som ersttning fr dremot fullt svarande vederlag i pengar eller pengars vrde.</SPAN></P>

<DIV id="id_4_2">
<P class="p14 ft9">Artikel 18</P>
<P class="p45 ft4">Offentlig tjnst</P>
<P class="p170 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft10">a) Ln och annan liknande ersttning, med undantag fr sdan inkomst som avses i artikel 17, som betalas av en avtalsslutande stat, en av dess politiska underavdelningar eller lokala myndigheter till fysisk person p grund av arbete som utfrts i denna stats, underavdel-</SPAN></P>
</DIV>
</DIV>
</DIV>
<DIV id="page_29">


<DIV id="id_1">
<DIV id="id_1_1">
<P class="p56 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft10">However, such salaries, wages and other similar remuneration shall be taxable only in the other Contracting State if the services are rendered in that State and the individual is a resident of that State who:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p171 ft3">(i) is a national of that State; or</P>
<P class="p172 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">(ii)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft10">did not become a resident of that State solely for the purpose of rendering the services.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p173 ft12"><SPAN class="ft3">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft14">The provisions of Article 14, 15 and 16 shall apply to salaries, wages, and other similar remuneration in respect of services rendered in connection with a business carried on by a Contracting State or a political subdivision or a local authority thereof.</SPAN></P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_1_2">
<P class="p112 ft3">nings eller myndighets tjnst, be- Prop. 2021/22:21 skattas endast i denna stat.</P>
<P class="p63 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft10">Sdan ln och annan liknande ersttning beskattas emellertid endast i den andra avtalsslutande staten om arbetet utfrs i denna andra stat och personen i frga har hemvist i denna stat och:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p174 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">1)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft10">r medborgare i denna stat,</SPAN></P>
<P class="p14 ft3">eller</P>
<P class="p67 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">2)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft10">inte fick hemvist i denna stat uteslutande fr att utfra arbetet,</SPAN></P>
<P class="p175 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft11">Bestmmelserna i artiklarna 14, 15 och 16 tillmpas p ln och annan liknande ersttning som betalas p grund av arbete som utfrts</SPAN></P>
<P class="p176 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">i</SPAN><SPAN class="ft10">samband med rrelse som bedrivs av en avtalsslutande stat, en av dess politiska underavdelningar eller lokala myndigheter.</SPAN></P>
</DIV>

<P class="p177 ft12"><SPAN class="ft3">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft14">In respect of grants, scholarships and other similar remuneration and remuneration from employment not covered by paragraph 1, a student or business apprentice referred to in paragraph 1 shall, in addition, be entitled during such education or training to the same exemptions, reliefs or reductions in</SPAN></P>

<P class="p178 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft11">Svitt avser bidrag, stipendier och liknande ersttningar, samt ersttning fr anstllning som inte omfattas av punkt 1, ska en studerande eller affrspraktikant som avses i nmnda punkt, under tiden fr sdan utbildning eller praktik, dessutom vara berttigad till</SPAN></P>

<P class="p89 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft11">Items of income of a resident of a Contracting State, wherever arising, not dealt with in the foregoing Articles of this Convention shall be taxable only in that State.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p98 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft11">The provisions of paragraph 1 shall not apply to income, other than income from immovable property as defined in paragraph 2 of Article 6, if the recipient of such income, being a resident of a Contracting State, carries on business in the other Contracting State through a permanent establishment situated therein and the right or property in respect of which the income is paid is effectively connected with such permanent establishment. In such case the provisions of Article 7 shall apply.</SPAN></P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_2_2">
<P class="p52 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">1.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft10">Inkomst som person med hemvist i en avtalsslutande stat frvrvar och som inte behandlas i fregende artiklar av detta avtal beskattas endast i denna stat, oavsett varifrn inkomsten hrrr.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p108 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft10">Bestmmelserna i punkt 1 tillmpas inte p inkomst, med undantag fr inkomst av fast egendom som avses i artikel 6 punkt 2, om mottagaren av inkomsten har hemvist i en avtalsslutande stat och bedriver rrelse i den andra avtalsslutande staten frn dr belget fast driftstlle samt den rttighet eller egendom i frga om vilken inkomsten betalas ger verkligt samband med det fasta driftstllet. I sdant fall tillmpas bestmmelserna i artikel 7.</SPAN></P>
</DIV>

<P class="p184 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">4.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft16">Alla andra slag av frmgenhet som en person med hemvist i en avtalsslutande stat innehar, beskattas endast i denna stat.</SPAN></P>

<DIV id="id_3">
<DIV id="id_3_1">
<P class="p14 ft4">Elimination of double taxation</P>
<P class="p185 ft3">Double taxation shall be eliminated as follows:</P>
<P class="p69 ft3">1. In Slovenia:</P>
<P class="p56 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft10">Where a resident of Slovenia derives income or owns capital which, in accordance with the provisions of this Convention, may be taxed in Sweden, Slovenia shall allow:</SPAN></P>
<P class="p186 ft3">(i) as deduction from the tax on the income of that resident, an amount equal to the income tax paid in Sweden;</P>
<P class="p186 ft3">(ii) as a deduction from the tax on the capital of that resident, an amount equal to the capital tax paid in Sweden.</P>
<P class="p62 ft3">Such deduction in either case shall not, however, exceed that part of the income tax or capital tax, as computed before the deduction is given, which is attributable, as the case may be, to the income or the capital which may be taxed in Sweden.</P>
<P class="p187 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft10">Where in accordance with any provision of the Convention income derived or capital owned by a resident of Slovenia is exempt from tax in Slovenia, Slovenia may nevertheless, in calculating the</SPAN></P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_3_2">
<P class="p14 ft4">Undvikande av dubbelbeskattning</P>

<P class="p69 ft3">1. I Slovenien:</P>
<P class="p63 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft10">Om en person med hemvist i Slovenien frvrvar inkomst eller innehar frmgenhet som enligt bestmmelserna i detta avtal fr beskattas i Sverige, ska Slovenien:</SPAN></P>

	<TD class="tr4 td112"><SPAN class="p3 ft2">&nbsp;</SPAN> </TD>

<P class="p188 ft3">Prop. 2021/22:21 amount of tax on the remaining income or capital of such resident, take into account the exempted income or capital.</P>
<P class="p189 ft3">2. In Sweden:</P>
<P class="p190 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft11">Where a resident of Sweden derives income which under the laws of Slovenia and in accordance with the provisions of this Convention may be taxed in Slovenia, Sweden shall allow  subject to the provisions of the laws of Sweden concerning credit for foreign tax (as they may be amended from time to time without changing the general principle hereof)  as a deduction from the tax on such income, an amount equal to the Slovenian tax paid in respect of such income.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p191 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft11">Where a resident of Sweden derives income which, in accordance with the provisions of this Convention, shall be taxable only in Slovenia, Sweden may, when determining the graduated rate of Swedish tax, take into account the income which shall be taxable only in Slovenia.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p192 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">c)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft11">Notwithstanding the provisions of </SPAN><NOBR>sub-paragraph</NOBR> a) of this paragraph, dividends paid by a company which is a resident of Slovenia to a company which is a resident of Sweden shall be exempt from Swedish tax according to the provisions of Swedish law governing the exemption of tax on dividends paid to Swedish companies by companies abroad.</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_1_2">
<P class="p193 ft3">lande av skatten p vrig inkomst eller frmgenhet beakta den inkomst eller frmgenhet som undantagits frn beskattning i Slovenien.</P>
<P class="p194 ft3">2. I Sverige:</P>
<P class="p195 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft10">Om en person med hemvist i Sverige frvrvar inkomst som enligt lagstiftning i Slovenien och i enlighet med bestmmelserna i detta avtal fr beskattas i Slovenien, ska Sverige  med beaktande av bestmmelserna i svensk lagstiftning betrffande avrkning av utlndsk skatt (ven i den lydelse de framledes kan f genom att ndras utan att den allmnna princip som anges hr ndras)  frn den svenska skatten p inkomsten avrkna ett belopp motsvarande den skatt i Slovenien som erlagts p inkomsten.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p196 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft10">Om en person med hemvist i Sverige frvrvar inkomst som i enlighet med detta avtal beskattas endast i Slovenien, fr Sverige, vid faststllande av skattesatsen fr svensk progressiv skatt beakta den inkomst som ska beskattas endast i Slovenien.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p197 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">c)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft10">Utan hinder av bestmmelserna i punkt a) i denna punkt r utdelning frn bolag med hemvist i Slovenien till bolag med hemvist i Sverige undantagen frn svensk skatt enligt bestmmelserna i svensk lag om skattebefrielse fr utdelning som erhlles av svenska bolag frn dotterbolag utomlands.</SPAN></P>

<DIV id="id_1">
<DIV id="id_1_1">
<P class="p89 ft12"><SPAN class="ft3">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft14">The competent authority shall endeavour, if the objection appears to it to be justified and if it is not itself able to arrive at a satisfactory solution, to resolve the case by mutual agreement with the competent authority of the other Contracting State, with a view to the avoidance of taxation which is not in accordance with the Convention. Any agreement reached shall be implemented notwithstanding any time limits in the domestic law of the Contracting States.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p201 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">3.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft10">The competent authorities of the Contracting States shall endeavour to resolve by mutual agreement any difficulties or doubts arising as to the interpretation or application of the Convention. They may also consult together for the elimination of double taxation in cases not provided for in the Convention.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p202 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">4.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft10">The competent authorities of the Contracting States may communicate with each other directly for the purpose of reaching an agreement in the sense of the preceding paragraphs.</SPAN></P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_1_2">
<P class="p203 ft3">Prop. 2021/22:21</P>
<P class="p204 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft11">Om den behriga myndigheten finner invndningen grundad men inte sjlv kan f till stnd en tillfredsstllande lsning, ska myndigheten ska lsa frgan genom msesidig verenskommelse med den behriga myndigheten i den andra avtalsslutande staten i syfte att undvika beskattning som strider mot avtalet. verenskommelse som trffats ska genomfras utan hinder av tidsgrnser i de avtalsslutande staternas interna lagstiftning.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p205 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">3.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft11">De behriga myndigheterna i de avtalsslutande staterna ska genom msesidig verenskommelse ska avgra svrigheter eller tvivelsml som uppkommer i frga om tolkningen eller tillmpningen av avtalet. De kan ven verlgga i syfte att undanrja dubbelbeskattning i fall som inte omfattas av avtalet.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p206 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">4.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft11">De behriga myndigheterna i de avtalsslutande staterna kan trda</SPAN></P>
<P class="p207 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">i</SPAN><SPAN class="ft11">direkt frbindelse med varandra i syfte att trffa verenskommelse i de fall som angivits i fregende punkter.</SPAN></P>

<DIV id="id_1_1">
<P class="p208 ft3">Prop. 2021/22:21 Convention. The exchange of information is not restricted by Articles 1 and 2.</P>
<P class="p209 ft12">2. Any information received under paragraph 1 by a Contracting State shall be treated as secret in the same manner as information obtained under the domestic laws of that State and shall be disclosed only to persons or authorities (including courts and administrative bodies) concerned with the assessment or collection of, the enforcement or prosecution in respect of, the determination of appeals in relation to the taxes referred to in paragraph 1, or the oversight of the above. Such persons or authorities shall use the information only for such purposes. They may disclose the information in public court proceedings or in judicial decisions. Notwithstanding the foregoing, information received by a Contracting State may be used for other purposes when such information may be used for such other purposes under the laws of both States and the competent authority of the supplying State authorises such use.</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_1_2">
<P class="p210 ft3">inte strider mot avtalet. Utbytet av upplysningar begrnsas inte av artiklarna 1 och 2.</P>
<P class="p53 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft10">Upplysningar som en avtalsslutande stat tagit emot enligt punkt 1 ska behandlas som hemliga p samma stt som upplysningar som erhllits enligt den interna lagstiftningen i denna stat och fr yppas endast fr personer eller myndigheter (dri inbegripet domstolar och frvaltningsorgan) som faststller, uppbr eller driver in de skatter som syftas i punkt 1 eller handlgger tal eller verklagande i frga om dessa skatter eller som utvar tillsyn ver nmnda verksamheter. Dessa personer eller myndigheter fr anvnda upplysningar bara fr sdana ndaml. De fr yppa upplysningarna vid offentlig rttegng eller i domstolsavgranden. Utan hinder av ovanstende fr upplysningar som en avtalsslutande stat mottagit anvndas fr andra ndaml nr sdana upplysningar fr anvndas fr sdana andra ndaml enligt lagstiftningen i bda avtalsslutande staterna och den behriga myndigheten i den avtalsslutande stat som lmnat upplysningarna tilltit sdant anvndande.</SPAN></P>

<P class="p89 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">5.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft10">In no case shall the provisions of paragraph 3 be construed to permit a Contracting State to decline to supply information solely because the information is held by a bank, other financial institution, nominee or person acting in an agency or a fiduciary capacity or because it relates to ownership interests in a person.</SPAN></P>

<DIV id="id_2_2">
<P class="p46 ft3">1. Utan hinder av vriga bestmmelser i detta avtal ska en frmn enligt avtalet inte ges i frga om en inkomst eller frmgenhetstillgng, om det med hnsyn till alla relevanta fakta och omstndigheter rimligen kan antas att ett av de huvudsakliga syftena med det arrangemang eller den transaktion som direkt eller indirekt resulterade i frmnen var att f frmnen, svida det inte faststlls att det under omstndigheterna r frenligt med de relevanta bestmmelsernas ndaml och syfte att frmnen ges.</P>
<P class="p214 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">2.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft10">Utan hinder av vriga bestmmelser i detta avtal, ska fr det fall a) bolag med hemvist i en avtalsslutande stat huvudsakligen frvrvar sina inkomster frn andra</SPAN></P>
<P class="p151 ft3">stater</P>
<P class="p215 ft3">1) frn <NOBR>bank-,</NOBR> <NOBR>sjfarts-,</NOBR> <NOBR>finans-,</NOBR> eller frskringsverksamhet, eller</P>
<P class="p216 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">2)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft10">genom att vara huvudkontor, </SPAN><NOBR>co-ordination</NOBR> centre eller en liknande enhet som tillhandahller administrativa eller andra tjnster till en grupp av bolag som bedriver rrelse huvudsakligen i andra stater; och</P>
<P class="p217 ft3">b) sdan inkomst beskattas vsentligt lgre enligt lagstiftningen i denna stat n inkomster frn liknande verksamhet som bedrivs inom denna stat eller genom att vara huvudkontor, <NOBR>co-ordination</NOBR> centre eller liknande enhet som tillhandahller administrativa eller andra tjnster till en grupp av bolag som bedriver rrelse i denna stat,</P>
<P class="p218 ft3">bestmmelserna i detta avtal som medfr undantag frn eller be-</P>
</DIV>
</DIV>
</DIV>
<DIV id="page_39">


<DIV id="id_1">
<DIV id="id_1_1">
<P class="p54 ft12">tion of tax shall not apply to the income of such company and to the dividends paid by such company.</P>
</DIV>

<P class="p14 ft3">grnsning av beskattningen inte Prop. 2021/22:21 tillmpas p inkomst som sdant</P>
<P class="p55 ft3">bolag frvrvar och inte heller p utdelning som betalas av sdant bolag.</P>

<P class="p127 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">3.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft10">Notwithstanding the provisions of paragraph 2, the provisions of Article 24 (Mutual agreement procedure) and Article 25 (Ex- change of information) shall have effect from the date of entry into force of this Convention, without regard to the taxable period to which the matter relates.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p144 ft12"><SPAN class="ft3">4.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft14">The Convention between the Socialist Federal Republic of Yugoslavia and the Kingdom of Sweden for the avoidance of double taxation with respect to taxes on</SPAN></P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_3_2">
<P class="p103 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">3.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft11">Utan hinder av bestmmelserna i punkt 2 ska bestmmelserna</SPAN></P>
<P class="p219 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">i</SPAN><SPAN class="ft11">artikel 24 (Frfarandet vid msesidig verenskommelse) och artikel 25 (Utbyte av upplysningar) tillmpas frn och med den dag d avtalet trder i kraft, oavsett vilket beskattningsr rendet gller.</SPAN></P>
<P class="p220 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">4.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft11">Avtalet mellan den Socialistiska Federala Republiken Jugoslavien och Konungariket Sverige fr att undvika dubbelbeskattning</SPAN></P>
<TABLE cellpadding=0 cellspacing=0 class="t20">
<TR>
	<TD class="tr5 td111"><SPAN class="p3 ft3">betrffande skatter p inkomst och</SPAN> </TD>
	<TD class="tr5 td112"><SPAN class="p17 ft3">39</SPAN> </TD>
</TR>
</TABLE>
</DIV>
</DIV>

<DIV id="page_40">


<DIV id="id_1">
<DIV id="id_1_1">
<P class="p90 ft3">Prop. 2021/22:21 income and capital, signed at Stockholm on 18<SPAN class="ft20">th </SPAN>June 1980 (the prior Convention), shall cease to have effect between Slovenia and Sweden with respect to any tax on the date upon which this Convention has effect with respect to that tax in accordance with the provisions of paragraph 2.</P>
<P class="p221 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">5.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft11">Notwithstanding the provisions of paragraphs 2 and 4 and the provisions of Article 17, where, immediately before the entry into force of this Convention, an individual was in receipt of payments falling within paragraphs 1, 2 and 3 of Article 18 of the prior Convention, that individual may make an election that the provisions of that Article, and not the provisions of Article 17 of this Convention, shall continue to apply to those payments. That election shall have effect for the year in which it is made and for subsequent years unless revoked by the individual. Where an election has been so revoked, no further election under this paragraph may be made.</SPAN></P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_1_2">
<P class="p54 ft3">frmgenhet, undertecknat i Stockholm den 18 juni 1980 (det tidigare avtalet) ska upphra att tillmpas mellan Slovenien och Sverige med avseende p varje skatt frn och med den dag d detta avtal enligt punkt 2 i denna artikel ska tillmpas avseende den aktuella skatten.</P>
<P class="p222 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">5.</SPAN><SPAN class="ft10">Utan hinder av bestmmelserna i punkterna 2 och 4 och bestmmelserna i artikel 17, fr en fysisk person som omedelbart fre avtalets ikrafttrdande var mottagare av sdana utbetalningar som omfattas av artikel 18 punkterna 1, 2 och 3 i det tidigare avtalet, vlja att bestmmelserna i sistnmnda artiklar och inte bestmmelserna i artikel 17 i detta avtal, fortfarande ska tillmpas p dessa utbetalningar. Detta val ska glla fr det r under vilket valet grs och varje drp fljande r under frutsttning att valet inte har terkallats av personen. Nr ett val har terkallats fr inte ett nytt val gras enligt denna punkt.</SPAN></P>
</DIV>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_2">
<DIV id="id_2_1">
<P class="p155 ft9">Article 29</P>
<P class="p156 ft4">Termination</P>
<P class="p223 ft3">This Convention shall remain in force until terminated by a Contracting State. Either Contracting State may terminate the Convention, through diplomatic channels, by giving written notice of termination at least six months before the end of any calendar year. In such case, the Convention shall cease to have effect:</P>
<P class="p224 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft11">in respect of taxes withheld at source, for amounts paid or credited on or after the first day of January of the calendar year next following the end of the </SPAN><NOBR>six-month</NOBR></P>
<P class="p225 ft3">40<SPAN style="padding-left:106px;">period;</SPAN></P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_2_2">
<P class="p14 ft9">Artikel 29</P>
<P class="p45 ft4">Upphrande</P>
<P class="p226 ft3">Detta avtal frblir i kraft till dess att det sgs upp av en avtalsslutande stat. Vardera avtalsslutande staten kan p diplomatisk vg skriftligen sga upp avtalet genom underrttelse hrom minst sex mnader fre utgngen av ngot kalenderr. I hndelse av sdan uppsgning upphr avtalet att glla:</P>
<P class="p227 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">a)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft10">i frga om kllskatter, p belopp som betalas eller tillgodofrs den 1 januari det kalenderr som fljer nrmast efter utgngen av sexmnadersperioden eller senare,</SPAN></P>
</DIV>
</DIV>
</DIV>
<DIV id="page_41">


<DIV id="id_1">
<DIV id="id_1_1">
<P class="p56 ft3"><SPAN class="ft3">b)</SPAN><SPAN class="ft10">in respect of other taxes on income, and taxes on capital, on taxes chargeable for any tax year beginning on or after the first day of January of the calendar year next following the end of the </SPAN><NOBR>six-month</NOBR> period.</P>
<P class="p228 ft3">IN WITNESS WHEREOF the undersigned, being duly authorized thereto, have signed this Convention.</P>

<P class="p165 ft3">b) i frga om andra skatter p in- Prop. 2021/22:21 komst och p frmgenhet, p skatt</P>
<P class="p231 ft3">som pfrs fr beskattningsr som brjar 1 januari det kalenderr som fljer nrmast efter utgngen av sexmnadersperioden eller senare.</P>
<P class="p232 ft3">Till bekrftelse hrav har undertecknade, drtill vederbrligen bemyndigade, undertecknat detta avtal.</P>

<DIV id="id_3_1">
<P class="p89 ft3">It is understood that should Sweden in the future introduce a tax on capital, the Convention shall apply to such tax. In such case double taxation shall be eliminated as follows:</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_3_2">
<P class="p234 ft3">Det r frsttt att fr det fallet Sverige i framtiden infr frmgenhetsskatt, s ska avtalet vara tillmpligt p denna skatt. Dubbelbeskattning ska i s fall undanrjas enligt fljande:</P>
<P class="p235 ft3">41</P>
</DIV>
</DIV>
</DIV>
<DIV id="page_42">


<DIV id="id_1">
<DIV id="id_1_1">
<P class="p90 ft3">Prop. 2021/22:21 Where a resident of Sweden owns capital which, in accordance with the provisions of the Convention, may be taxed in Slovenia, Sweden shall allow as a deduction from the tax on the capital of that resident an amount equal to the capital tax paid in Slovenia. Such deduction shall not, however, exceed that part of the Swedish capital tax, as computed before the deduction is given, which is attributable to the capital which may be taxed in Slovenia.</P>
</DIV>
<DIV id="id_1_2">
<P class="p89 ft3">Om en person med hemvist i Sverige innehar frmgenhet, som enligt bestmmelserna i detta avtal fr beskattas i Slovenien, ska Sverige frn skatten p denna persons frmgenhet avrkna ett belopp motsvarande den frmgenhetsskatt som erlagts i Slovenien. Avrkningsbeloppet ska emellertid inte verstiga den del av den svenska frmgenhetsskatten, berknad utan sdan avrkning, som belper p den frmgenhet som fr beskattas i Slovenien.</P>

<P class="p14 ft4">4. With reference to Article 13:</P>
<P class="p172 ft3">With respect to gains derived by the air transport consortium Scandinavian Airlines System (SAS), the provisions of paragraph 3 of Article 13 of the Convention shall apply only to such part of the gains as corresponds to the participation held in that consortium by SAS Sverige AB, the Swedish partner of SAS.</P>
